  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_949f0976-fee9-415d-931a-04b72b8560c8'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };
    if (typeof AppleID !== "undefined") {
      initAppleId();
    } else {
      initializeSiwa();
    }
  //]]>
</script>

      <div id="description" class="readable stacked" style="right:0">
        
<span id="freeTextContainer9978842225220286963">"للمرة الثانية بعد "فيرتيجو" يتّخذ أحمد مراد من الجريمة خلفية تكشف بأسلوب مشوّق كواليس المجتمع و الفساد المستشري وسط كل طبقاته.. وهو بذلك يؤّكد قواعد النوع الروائي الذي أصبح رائدًا له".. <br/>صنع الله إبراهيم<br/>لم يكن "طه" سوى مندوب دعاية طبية في شركة أدوية؛ حياة باهتة رتيبة، بدلة و كرافتة و حقيبة جلدية و لسان لبق يستميل أعتى الأطباء لأدويته<br/>وفي البيت يعيش وحيدًا مع أبيه القعيد<br/>كان </span>
  <span id="freeText9978842225220286963" style="display:none">"للمرة الثانية بعد "فيرتيجو" يتّخذ أحمد مراد من الجريمة خلفية تكشف بأسلوب مشوّق كواليس المجتمع و الفساد المستشري وسط كل طبقاته.. وهو بذلك يؤّكد قواعد النوع الروائي الذي أصبح رائدًا له".. <br />صنع الله إبراهيم<br />لم يكن "طه" سوى مندوب دعاية طبية في شركة أدوية؛ حياة باهتة رتيبة، بدلة و كرافتة و حقيبة جلدية و لسان لبق يستميل أعتى الأطباء لأدويته<br />وفي البيت يعيش وحيدًا مع أبيه القعيد<br />كان ذلك قبل أن تقع جريمة قتل غامضة تتركه خلفها و قد تبدّل عالمه.. للأبد<br />تتحول حياته إلى جزيرة من الأسرار، يبدأ اكتشافها في دفتر عتيق يعثر عليه مصادفة، و يجد معه أداة رهيبة لها فعل السحر<br />عندها يبدأ "طه" ومعه الضابط "وليد سلطان" في تتبع قاتل لا يملكان دليلا ضده<br />سنقرأ هنا كيف تتحول هذه الجريمة إلى سلسلة من عمليات القتل. وكيف يصبح القتل بابًا يكشف لنا عالما من الفساد، وسطوة السلطة التي تمتد لأجيال في تتابع مثير لا يؤكد أبدا أن "طه" سيصل إلى نهايته<br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.titaniumstores.com/dp/9770927627">http://www.titaniumstores.com/dp/9770...</a></span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/413478443" />
    <a title="Engi Amin" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6455519-engi-amin"><img alt="Engi Amin" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1356821537p2/6455519.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/413478443?book_show_action=true">Sep 13, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Engi Amin" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Engi Amin" href="/user/show/6455519-engi-amin">Engi Amin</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9789770927625" href="/book/show/13445299">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer413478443" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6703195476836990072">Hmmmm.. How shall I start..<br/><br/>It's good, no doubt, in terms of creativity and evolution of events. I totally loved the creativity of the idea. Ahmed Mourad did an incredible effort researching and preparing for it. Diamond Dust. I bet no one who had read this novel didn't google about diamond dust! :D Found no satisfying results though, just like Taha stated! (Taha: the protagonist of the novel)<br/><br/>Another interesting thing about it was the idea of taking justice into one's own hand and justifying murd</span>
  <span id="freeText6703195476836990072" style="display:none">Hmmmm.. How shall I start..<br /><br />It's good, no doubt, in terms of creativity and evolution of events. I totally loved the creativity of the idea. Ahmed Mourad did an incredible effort researching and preparing for it. Diamond Dust. I bet no one who had read this novel didn't google about diamond dust! :D Found no satisfying results though, just like Taha stated! (Taha: the protagonist of the novel)<br /><br />Another interesting thing about it was the idea of taking justice into one's own hand and justifying murder as a heavenly quest to "purge the evil". Makes me wonder if Mourad is fan of "Death Note" too.<br /><br />However ...<br /><br />Sara (the main female character)just didn't fit into place. I felt like she was forced into the plot to fill in an irrelevant role that, I think, the author wanted to convey a message through; but it just didn't fit into the core of the plot.<br /><br />Also, by the end of the story, I couldn't get a grip on the message Mourad was trying to convey through his piece of work. Something seemed missing or disengaged; or so I think, at least, in comparison to "Vertigo". The ending was just meh to me. <br /><br />Being a big fan of Mourad's work, I have to say i'm a little concerned about his repetitive approach in setting up the characters of his novels. There's always the male protagonist who leads a normal life at the beginning but then turns into a hero. The faithful, loyal, humorous friend. The female lover. The underrated parent figure. But I have to say that I do enjoy the different types of corrupted characters that always include a high ranked authority figure.</span>
  <a data-text-id="6703195476836990072" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer2624008631986066567">I would recommend this book to those who love crime books. It is a quick read and very interesting. I only gave it 3 stars cause I wasn't crazy about it. <br/>The story was well-built but there were parts that I got confused and couldn't totally understand what the author was meaning to say.<br/>Taha is the main protagonist, liked his character, how his father's death/murder completely turned his life upside down, from being a so typical pharmacist to the killer who wanted to avenge his father's death. I </span>
  <span id="freeText2624008631986066567" style="display:none">I would recommend this book to those who love crime books. It is a quick read and very interesting. I only gave it 3 stars cause I wasn't crazy about it. <br />The story was well-built but there were parts that I got confused and couldn't totally understand what the author was meaning to say.<br />Taha is the main protagonist, liked his character, how his father's death/murder completely turned his life upside down, from being a so typical pharmacist to the killer who wanted to avenge his father's death. I would do the same if I were him.<br />But I didn't like that his father decided to fulfill justice by killing bad guys on his own using diamond dust ((his secret weapon)).<br />He skipped telling the authorities and went after them. And the consequences were affecting both him and his son "I don't like waking up to find my father killing people/villains.<br />It would have been better if Ahmed/the author wrote a more believable plot not involving a disabled man and make him a serial killer-regardless his motives-.<br />Yasser-Taha's best friend- a character I truly adored. So funny and so helpful to taha. I liked their conversations together.. Made me giggling, they were so Egyptian style.<br />Sara Taha's neighbor which he had interest in her so did she. The more the character developed through out the events the more I disliked her. Eventually they ended up together but they weren't a match. But I wasn't so fond of the love story.<br /></span>

<div id="review_394862082" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/394862082" />
    <a title="Rania" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2949332-rania"><img alt="Rania" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1367335023p2/2949332.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/394862082?book_show_action=true">Aug 18, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Rania" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Rania" href="/user/show/2949332-rania">Rania</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer394862082" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10260407616209901926">After reading this book, I find it difficult to start reading any other book! It's become my best book of all times! Ahmed Mourad is just an amazing writer! I love his language, his style, his description of setting and characters, his unprecedented sense of humour, everything! The central character in this book is Taha, a 30-year-old medical rep who works for a medical company as well as in a pharmacy. His life has been monotonous since his father got paralyzed and his mother left home when he </span>
  <span id="freeText10260407616209901926" style="display:none">After reading this book, I find it difficult to start reading any other book! It's become my best book of all times! Ahmed Mourad is just an amazing writer! I love his language, his style, his description of setting and characters, his unprecedented sense of humour, everything! The central character in this book is Taha, a 30-year-old medical rep who works for a medical company as well as in a pharmacy. His life has been monotonous since his father got paralyzed and his mother left home when he was around 17. Suddenly, a series of murders turn his life upside down. The book sheds light on the corruption that was devouring the Egyptian society before the Revolution. Indeed, the book is a kind of "prequel" to the Revolution. We are introduced to rich corrupt people who appear to be innocent and respected, but who are, in fact, corrupt and indecent. Another central theme in the book is the corruption of the Egyptian police who abuse their power and use criminals in order to achieve their goals instead of protecting the society from them. There's also a romantic side of the novel, the interesting love story we have of Taha and Sara, a feminist, courageous journalist who joins demonstrations and who is an example of an extraordinary Egyptian girl. An excellent read indeed!</span>
  <a data-text-id="10260407616209901926" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('ZLwEs6uOhalpTAQ52cFWwHHIZtqHnzvGOWYqLYtZP9Zemm1hENBMwc5nsFguNFwfp5eBEkkStaFiGGycRhrNTA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('EFnNx12Ew/lCjCFhCj3LwwiA0UdD0jbfs2jAaWB9KwAqf6QV5toKkeWnlQD9yMEc3t82j41fuLjoFobYrT7Zmg==')})
  }
//]]>

      <div id="aboutAuthor" class=" clearFloats bigBox"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground"><a href="/author/show/1633682._">About أحمد مراد</a></h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent">
          <div class='bookAuthorProfile'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__topContainer'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__photoContainer'>
<a href="/author/show/1633682._"><div class='bookAuthorProfile__photo' style='background-image: url(https://images.gr-assets.com/authors/1227520027p3/1633682.jpg);'></div>

followers

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer4060736643893888542">أحمد مراد.. <br/>كاتب مصري من مواليد القاهرة 1978، تخرّج في مدرسة ليسيه الحرّية بباب اللوق عام 2006 قبل أن يلتحق بالمعهد العالي للسينما ليدرس التصوير السينمائي، وتخرّج عام 2001 بترتيب الأول على القسم، ونالت أفلام تخرّجه "الهائمون - الثلاث ورقات - وفي اليوم السابع" جوائز للأفلام القصيرة في مهرجانات بإنجلترا وفرنسا وأوكرانيا.. <br/>بدأ أحمد كتابة روايته الأولي "فيرتيجو" في شتاء عام 2007، ونُشِرت في نفس العام </span>
  <span id="freeText4060736643893888542" style="display:none">أحمد مراد.. <br />كاتب مصري من مواليد القاهرة 1978، تخرّج في مدرسة ليسيه الحرّية بباب اللوق عام 2006 قبل أن يلتحق بالمعهد العالي للسينما ليدرس التصوير السينمائي، وتخرّج عام 2001 بترتيب الأول على القسم، ونالت أفلام تخرّجه "الهائمون - الثلاث ورقات - وفي اليوم السابع" جوائز للأفلام القصيرة في مهرجانات بإنجلترا وفرنسا وأوكرانيا.. <br />بدأ أحمد كتابة روايته الأولي "فيرتيجو" في شتاء عام 2007، ونُشِرت في نفس العام عن دار "ميريت"، قبل أن تُترجم للّغة الإنجليزية عن دار "بلومزبيري"، ثم للإيطالية عن دار "مارسيليو"، والفرنسية عن دار "فلاماريون".. ثم تحولت الرواية لمسلسل تليفزيوني في رمضان من عام 2012.. <br />ثم أصدر أحمد روايته الثانية في فبراير 2010 بعنوان "تراب الماس" وتُرجمت للإيطالية عن دار "مارسيليو"، وأتبعها برواية "الفيل الأزرق" التي صدرت في أكتوبر من عام 2012.. </span>
